BEGIN BEGIN  wight of wildling girl END END BEGIN BEGIN he also finds a DEAD wildling girl pinned to a tree END END BEGIN BEGIN he reports back to the others END END BEGIN BEGIN ser WAYMAR overrides the older GARED 'S advice that they return to CASTLE BLACK to report the situation to their superiors and instead insists on seeing the corpses for himself  to determine what killed them END END BEGIN BEGIN when they reach the site  the bodies have disappeared END END BEGIN BEGIN will scouts around for clues  but GARED finds a bloody piece of clothing buried under the SNOW END END BEGIN BEGIN further investigations are curtailed when a tall  humanoid figure with glowing blue eyes  a WHITE WALKER  arrives and KILLS ser WAYMAR with ease END END BEGIN BEGIN GARED attempts to escape but is caught and killed END END BEGIN BEGIN will  in extreme horror  sees the DEAD wildling girl from earlier now walking with blue eyes  and also witnesses GARED 'S death  with the WHITE WALKER tossing his severed head at will 's feet END END

BEGIN BEGIN BENJEN STARK meets JON atop the WALL and tells him he is going on a ranging in the haunted FOREST END END BEGIN BEGIN he refuses to take JON with him  telling him he isn 't ready  and that here rank and nobility mean nothing every MAN must earn everything he gets END END BEGIN BEGIN before departing  BENJEN stops by the eating area to farewell YOREN  a fellow NIGHT 'S watchman who scouts for NEW recruits in the capital END END BEGIN BEGIN BENJEN also scolds TYRION for his naivety regarding what is NORTH of the WALL and states that TYRION has no authority to say what is or isn 't BEYOND the WALL as he hasn 't been out there himself END END 
BEGIN BEGIN later  TYRION discusses NORTH of the WALL with JEOR MORMONT and his chief adviser  the ancient and blind maester AEMON END END BEGIN BEGIN JEOR asks for TYRION to intercede at court and get the WATCH more MEN as they are dangerously undermanned END END BEGIN BEGIN AEMON warns that the STARK WORDS are right a terrible WINTER is COMING and more dangerous THINGS than just WILDLINGS might COME with it after all  one of their number swore that the WHITE WALKERS had returned .. END END BEGIN BEGIN right up to the moment NED STARK cut his head off END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION admits his skepticism that supernatural creatures might exist  but he agrees to bring word to his queen END END 
BEGIN BEGIN before departing for king 's LANDING  TYRION fulfils an OLD ambition by climbing to the top of the WALL and urinating off the edge of it END END BEGIN BEGIN he and JON share a moment of fellowship before TYRION departs for the capital in the company of YOREN END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS commands the KHALASAR to halt on a whim  exercising her growing authority and power END END BEGIN BEGIN VISERYS does not take well to being commanded and threatens his sister END END BEGIN BEGIN he is strangled by RAKHARO  a DOTHRAKI warrior wielding a whip END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS calms the situation and VISERYS is forced to WALK  a sign of shame amongst the horse riding DOTHRAKI END END BEGIN BEGIN later  IRRI reveals to DAENERYS that DAENERYS is pregnant END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS relays the NEWS to KHAL DROGO and tells him she thinks it will be a BOY as they lie naked in each other 's arms END END BEGIN BEGIN ser JORAH MORMONT and RAKHARO compare the westerosi and DOTHRAKI ways of BATTLE the heavily armored but slow KNIGHTS versus the lightly armored but fast moving horse warriors END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH has heard of RAKHARO 'S father  a GREAT warrior  but admits that he disgraced his own father  a MAN of GREAT HONOR END END BEGIN BEGIN when he learns that DAENERYS is pregnant  he announces he must split off from the column to ride to the FREE CITY of qohor  but will rejoin them before they reach VAES DOTHRAK END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  lord SNOW is the third EPISODE of the FIRST SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the third EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it FIRST aired on MAY 1  2011 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by executive producers DAVID BENIOFF D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS and directed by brian kirk END END 
BEGIN BEGIN JON SNOW attempts to find his footing at CASTLE BLACK amidst hostility and suspicion from his fellow members of the NIGHT 'S WATCH END END BEGIN BEGIN EDDARD STARK and his daughters arrive at king 's LANDING END END BEGIN BEGIN CATELYN renews an OLD friendship with a member of the court  while DAENERYS and VISERYS journey onwards to the DOTHRAKI capital of VAES DOTHRAK END END 
BEGIN BEGIN TYRION speaks with BRAN END END BEGIN BEGIN in WINTERFELL  BRAN STARK has a nightmare in which he sees a THREE EYED RAVEN  sitting on one of the STONE direwolves OUTSIDE the doorway to the STARK crypts END END BEGIN BEGIN he wakes up to find his direwolf SUMMER by his side END END BEGIN BEGIN THEON GREYJOY summons HODOR  the CASTLE 'S dim witted stableboy  who can only say the word HODOR  to help carry BRAN down to the GREAT HALL  where ROBB STARK is hosting a meeting with TYRION LANNISTER and YOREN  both traveling down from the WALL to king 's LANDING together END END BEGIN BEGIN ROBB very pointedly offers hospitality to any MAN of the WATCH  silently letting TYRION know he is not invited to stay at WINTERFELL END END 
BEGIN BEGIN when BRAN arrives  TYRION sympathizes with BRAN for being a cripple  which annoys BRAN  as does asking him if he likes to ride  but TYRION simply says it is the truth  no less so for being a hard truth END END BEGIN BEGIN he gives the STARKS the design of a saddle which will allow BRAN to ride even in his current state END END BEGIN BEGIN he does it to repay BRAN 'S half brother 's friendship and because he has a weakness for  CRIPPLES  BASTARDS and BROKEN THINGS END END BEGIN BEGIN due to this kindness  ROBB says he can stay  but TYRION says he would prefer the brothel in TOWN END END BEGIN BEGIN while preparing to leave the CASTLE  THEON COMES to TYRION and rather condescendingly sends him off  recommending the prostitute ros at the brothel END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION asks THEON why lady CATELYN was not present to receive him and concludes that CATELYN is not in WINTERFELL END END BEGIN BEGIN he also taunts THEON about how the son of the ferocious BALON GREYJOY has been reduced to playing lackey in WINTERFELL to his captors  which infuriates THEON and gives him a coin  assuming that he has not already had sex with ros END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at CASTLE BLACK  a NEW recruit for the NIGHT 'S WATCH has arrived SAMWELL TARLY  the son of the famous lord randyll TARLY END END BEGIN BEGIN SAMWELL is fat  soft and pampered  and in his FIRST practice fight does dismally END END BEGIN BEGIN ser ALLISER THORNE has no time for his weakness END END BEGIN BEGIN he directs the other recruits to attack 'ser PIGGY '  but JON SNOW finds this cruel and unfair  and takes pity on SAM and fends off the attackers END END BEGIN BEGIN THORNE tries to turn it into a GAME  ordering THREE trainees take on SAM 'S PROTECTOR taunting JON that he has found a NEW lady love  but JON nevertheless fends them all off END END BEGIN BEGIN SAMWELL is naive and self deprecating  claiming to be a coward and craven  to JON 'S astonishment END END BEGIN BEGIN no one admits to being a coward  and GRENN says that they shouldn 't even be seen talking to him END END 
BEGIN BEGIN SAM joins JON on the WALL for sentry duty  even though he says his eyesight is weak  he is afraid of heights  and can 't take the cold END END BEGIN BEGIN JON asks why he joined the NIGHT 'S WATCH as he is afraid of everything END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM tells him that on his eighteenth nameday his father offered him a choice END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM was a MAN and his heir  but he was not skilled at combat  he was unworthy of his NAME and birthright END END BEGIN BEGIN samwall 's father forced him to join the NIGHT 'S WATCH  and told him that if he refused  he would arrange a hunting trip with his son in the WOODS  and implied that SAM would be killed in a way that looked accidental END END BEGIN BEGIN JON is shocked that a true born son of HIGH birth should be treated worse than he himself had been as a bastard END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM knows that the next day he will be made to fight again and expects it to be bad END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  GRENN yields to SAMWELL END END BEGIN BEGIN at the WALL  JON orders the recruits to go easy on SAM  but RAST refuses  saying that if ser ALLISER orders him to fight 'lady PIGGY '  he will slice himself off a side of bacon END END BEGIN BEGIN in response to RAST 'S comments  JON goes to his bed that NIGHT and uses his direwolf GHOST to intimidate RAST into playing along END END BEGIN BEGIN the next day  no one will fight SAM END END BEGIN BEGIN after GRENN takes a very weak blow from SAM and yields  ser ALLISER scolds JON for his rebellious actions END END BEGIN BEGIN later  when JON and SAM are cleaning the dining HALL  they talk about how neither of them have been with a WOMAN END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM tells JON that he has not had success with girls  while JON reveals he 'd rather not risk siring a child that will have the life of a bastard like himself END END BEGIN BEGIN a furious ALLISER THORNE COMES in and tells JON that this charity won 't help SAM harden up to survive the WINTER that is COMING END END BEGIN BEGIN he tells them the truly horrific experience he went through trapped by a blizzard NORTH of the WALL that ENDED in cannibalism END END 
BEGIN BEGIN KHAL DROGO 'S KHALASAR arrives at VAES DOTHRAK  the DOTHRAKI CITY END END BEGIN BEGIN there are no CITY WALLS  but there is a large gateway arch made of TWO statues of rearing horses END END BEGIN BEGIN VISERYS is annoyed that DROGO has been taking 'his ' ARMY in the wrong direction END END BEGIN BEGIN later  he bathes with DOREAH and tells her about how he was raised with stories about the TARGARYEN DRAGONS and his own destiny END END BEGIN BEGIN he recites the NAMES of SEVERAL DRAGONS  and tells her about the skulls of DRAGONS that once decorated the THRONE room at king 's LANDING  but she starts to annoy him with talk of DRAGONS  reminding him that they are DEAD END END BEGIN BEGIN he tells her to finish pleasuring him in silence END END 
BEGIN BEGIN VISERYS is enraged when DAENERYS sends DOREAH with an invite for him to dine with her  as he interprets this as his sister commanding him to COME END END BEGIN BEGIN he drags DOREAH into DAENERYS ' tent  and insults her dinner and the GIFTS of clothes she tries to give him END END BEGIN BEGIN he is still dressed in his now ragged clothes from PENTOS  having refused to dress like a DOTHRAKI  whom he regards as savage pordh END END BEGIN BEGIN he sneers that next she will try to braid his hair like a DOTHRAKI END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS retorts that he has no right to braid his hair until he is victorious in BATTLE  which further infuriates him END END BEGIN BEGIN in his anger  VISERYS tackles her to the ground and tries to strike her  calling her nothing but a horselord 's slut  and warning her that she 's awoken the dragon  but this time she fights back  hitting him in the face with a metal and leather belt END END BEGIN BEGIN she tells a thunderstruck VISERYS that she is the KHAL 'S wife  and is carrying his child and by implication  VISERYS is nothing to the DOTHRAKI  and warns that if he raises a HAND against her again  he will lose his HANDS END END BEGIN BEGIN later  DAENERYS confides in MORMONT her realization that VISERYS will NEVER become king of WESTEROS END END BEGIN BEGIN he is so weak and ineffectual that he couldn 't command an ARMY even if DROGO gave him one  to which JORAH agrees END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in the RED KEEP  SANSA STARK visits the GREAT HALL  where the IRON THRONE sits END END BEGIN BEGIN she and SEPTA MORDANE discuss the expectation that SANSA will have to provide JOFFREY with an heir END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA thinks the REALM will hate her if she only has daughters  along with her belief JOFFREY is still angry over the incident by the river and her anger at her father over lady 's death END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  the SMALL COUNCIL meets END END BEGIN BEGIN during a meeting of the SMALL COUNCIL  lord EDDARD learns that the forthcoming tournament to celebrate his appointment is seeing the CITY swell with visitors  and has already resulted in a tavern riot  a brothel FIRE  THREE stabbings and a drunken horse race END END BEGIN BEGIN he tells LITTLEFINGER that money will have to be found to strengthen the CITY guards  as well as giving twenty of his own MEN to JANOS SLYNT 'S command  until the tournament is over END END BEGIN BEGIN after the meeting EDDARD talks to GRAND maester PYCELLE about JON ARRYN 'S LAST few weeks END END BEGIN BEGIN PYCELLE said he did all he could to save JON ARRYN  but the illness was sudden and severe END END BEGIN BEGIN he recalls that shortly before his sudden illness  ARRYN had borrowed a truly boring BOOK about the lineages of the SEVEN KINGDOMS  and his LAST WORDS were  the seed is strong END END 
BEGIN BEGIN taking the BOOK with him  EDDARD COMES across ARYA in the HALL standing on one leg as part of her training with SYRIO END END BEGIN BEGIN ARYA asks whether BRAN would be able to live in king 's LANDING with them now that he 's awoken  but EDDARD states that he would have to regain his strength FIRST END END BEGIN BEGIN ARYA then comments that BRAN had always wanted to be a KNIGHT in the king 's guard  but will no longer be able to due to his paralysis END END BEGIN BEGIN EDDARD confirms this to be the case  but states that BRAN will be able to do many other THINGS such as become lord of a holdfast  sit on the king 's COUNCIL  or raise CASTLES END END BEGIN BEGIN when ARYA asks if she would be able to become any of those  EDDARD instead tells her that she will marry a highborn lord and have lords and PRINCES for SONS END END BEGIN BEGIN however  ARYA is not pleased with this response  telling her father  that 's not me END END BEGIN BEGIN she goes back to balancing on one leg as EDDARD looks on END END

BEGIN BEGIN JON is summoned to MORMONT 'S chambers as NEWS has arrived of EDDARD 'S arrest and imprisonment END END BEGIN BEGIN after being given the letter to read for himself  a speechless JON attempts to leave before MORMONT reminds him of the oath he has sworn to the NIGHT 'S WATCH END END BEGIN BEGIN when JON expresses concern for his SISTERS  MORMONT replies he is sure they are unharmed  though JON is doubtful END END 
BEGIN BEGIN later on  ALLISER THORNE taunts JON that his father is a traitor  calling him  not just a bastard  a traitor 's bastard END END BEGIN BEGIN JON angrily charges at him with a knife and THORNE is only saved by GRENN and PYP holding JON back END END BEGIN BEGIN commander MORMONT witnessed the incident and confines JON to quarters for his trouble END END BEGIN BEGIN that NIGHT  JON is aroused by a whining GHOST scratching at the DOOR END END BEGIN BEGIN sensing trouble  JON and his direwolf head to the lord commander 's chambers where JON is confronted by a wight  the reanimated corpse of the DEAD NIGHT 'S watchman END END BEGIN BEGIN though JON is able to stab the wight through the chest with his sword  the wight simply removes the sword and is unharmed END END BEGIN BEGIN MORMONT appears  seeking out the commotion END END BEGIN BEGIN JON grabs MORMONT 'S oil lamp and throws it at the wight  finally destroying it END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the morning after  the TWO wight bodies have been thoroughly burned END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM says he read in a BOOK that the DEAD are animated by the touch of the WHITE WALKERS and only FIRE can destroy such creatures END END BEGIN BEGIN he hopes the WALL is big enough to HOLD them back when the WALKERS COME in force END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at the EYRIE  CATELYN is furious with LYSA FIRST for LYSA not immediately notifying her about EDDARD 'S arrest and SECOND for refusing to consider summoning the KNIGHTS of the VALE to war END END BEGIN BEGIN despite setting in motion this chain of events with her letter to her sister regarding the murder of JON ARRYN  LYSA does not believe that war is in the VALE 'S best interests and rather want the KNIGHTS to stay in the VALE to protect her son and their lord END END 
BEGIN BEGIN TYRION and BRONN have reached the western edge of the VALE and are surrounded by members of the hill tribes  led by a fearsome warrior named SHAGGA END END BEGIN BEGIN at FIRST he orders them to be killed  but TYRION does some fast talking and convinces the hill tribes that HOUSE LANNISTER is an enemy of the HOUSE ARRYN and its rulers END END BEGIN BEGIN he proposes an alliance which will allow the tribes to enact vengeance against HOUSE ARRYN and take ownership of the LANDS of the VALE END END BEGIN BEGIN they eagerly agree  and escort TYRION and BRONN westwards towards where the LANNISTER armies are gathering END END 
BEGIN BEGIN dozens of RAVENS leaving WINTERFELL  summoning the BANNERS of the NORTH to war END END 
BEGIN BEGIN ROBB receives a letter from SANSA in king 's LANDING  asking him to pledge fealty to king JOFFREY END END BEGIN BEGIN maester LUWIN correctly deduces the letter is actually the work of the queen END END BEGIN BEGIN ROBB refuses to consider the request and sends out RAVENS  summoning the lords bannermen of the NORTH and their armies to assemble at WINTERFELL END END BEGIN BEGIN released RAVENS fill the sky END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at WINTERFELL  ROBB HOLDS a feast for SEVERAL of his newly arrived bannermen END END BEGIN BEGIN JON UMBER assumes that he will lead the vanguard  and is offended by the suggestion that he would be made to march behind a glover  threatening to withdraw from the host END END BEGIN BEGIN in response  ROBB promises that  after the conflict with the LANNISTERS  he will oust GREATJON from his KEEP and hang him for breaking his oaths to HOUSE STARK when the enraged bannerman goes to draw a weapon  ROBB 'S direwolf GREY WIND sets upon him  biting off TWO of his FINGERS END END BEGIN BEGIN ROBB recites 'that it is death to BEAR steel against your liege lord ' but then diffuses the situation by excusing GREATJON 'S aggression  saying that 'doubtless  the GREATJON only meant to cut my meat for me ' END END BEGIN BEGIN the GREATJON roars with laughter and accepts ROBB 'S commands  much to the shock of BRAN  who witnessed the entire incident END END BEGIN BEGIN ROBB says farewell to BRAN and to RICKON  who is convinced he 'll see neither ROBB nor his parents again END END 
BEGIN BEGIN BRAN prays by the heart tree when he is approached by OSHA who tells him the OLD GODS of the FOREST are listening to him and that the WILDLINGS also worship the OLD GODS END END BEGIN BEGIN she laments that the SOUTH has lost touch with the past the southern WEIRWOODS were cut down years ago and the southerners have no idea what 's awakening in the NORTH END END BEGIN BEGIN they are interrupted by HODOR who was bathing and has forgotten to put his clothes back on  and OSHA remarks that he might have giant BLOOD in him before BRAN sends him away END END BEGIN BEGIN curious  BRAN asks her if giants live BEYOND the WALL END END BEGIN BEGIN she affirms they do  as well has many other beings  though not all of them are friendly END END BEGIN BEGIN she asserts that the ARMY ROBB has gathered should be marching NORTH  not SOUTH END END

BEGIN BEGIN KEVAN and TYWIN LANNISTER greet TYRION and his companions END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION  BRONN  SHAGGA and the rest of the hill tribesmen arrive at the LANNISTER encampment  to find lord TYWIN LANNISTER and his brother  ser KEVAN  planning to engage the STARK ARMY  which is moving SOUTH from the NECK END END BEGIN BEGIN TYWIN shows no sign of relief that his son is alive END END BEGIN BEGIN TYWIN accepts the aid of the hill tribesmen  but SHAGGA will only fight if TYRION fights alongside them  a prospect which TYWIN welcomes and terrifies TYRION END END 
BEGIN BEGIN KHAL DROGO disciplines MAGO END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS notes DROGO 'S injury END END BEGIN BEGIN in essos  KHAL DROGO having taken an oath to take the IRON THRONE  has begun his march of conquest to the NARROW SEA END END BEGIN BEGIN the DOTHRAKI raid a village in lhazar  a peaceful country to the SOUTH east of VAES DOTHRAK END END BEGIN BEGIN to finance the war to COME  they must raid villages and take people to sell into slavery  thereby gaining the money to hire ships for the KHALASAR to assault WESTEROS END END BEGIN BEGIN ser JORAH and others try to explain this to DAENERYS  but she is disturbed to see the aftermath  the DOTHRAKI killing the villagers and raping their women  and orders it stopped END END BEGIN BEGIN the DOTHRAKI grow angry at not being able to take the spoils of victory  as that is the DOTHRAKI way END END BEGIN BEGIN she starts claiming all the women they see to protect them END END BEGIN BEGIN the angry warriors take their complaints to KHAL DROGO  but he is amused at his wife 's fierceness END END BEGIN BEGIN he tells them that DAENERYS MAY KEEP the women she has claimed  they can find others END END BEGIN BEGIN one MAN won 't listen  and angrily accuses DROGO of being slave to a foreign whore END END BEGIN BEGIN KHAL DROGO stops the complaints by killing MAGO  the offended warrior who challenges him END END BEGIN BEGIN DROGO takes a deep wound to the chest in the process END END BEGIN BEGIN though DROGO dismisses it as a scratch  DAENERYS insists it be treated and allows one of the women she rescued  a healer called MIRRI MAZ DUUR to treat the wound  despite the distaste of DROGO 'S bloodriders  who derisively call the WOMAN maegi a witch  END END

BEGIN BEGIN the child offers a GIFT to DAENERYS a wooden ball but as she picks it up  the hooded STRANGER knocks it out of her HANDS ser JORAH grabs the STRANGER and their struggle knocks DAENERYS to the ground  where to her horror  the ball cracks in half and a manticore emerges to attack END END BEGIN BEGIN before the creature can harm DAENERYS with its lethal sting  the STRANGER impales it with his dagger and charges at the child  who hisses in a reptilian manner  baring teeth and features reminiscent of PYAT PREE  and uses magic to escape END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS realizes the assassin was likely an agent of the surviving warlocks of QARTH END END 
BEGIN BEGIN turning her attention to her savior  DAENERYS is surprised when the MAN addresses her as his queen and removes his hood END END BEGIN BEGIN she asks if JORAH knows the MAN END END BEGIN BEGIN a stunned JORAH admits he does the STRANGER before them is one of the most skilled fighters in WESTEROS ser BARRISTAN SELMY  lord commander of ROBERT BARATHEON 'S KINGSGUARD END END BEGIN BEGIN falling to his knees  ser BARRISTAN explains that following ROBERT 'S death and his dismissal by JOFFREY  he has been searching for DAENERYS stormborn  to beg her forgiveness and offer his service  hoping to make amends for failing HOUSE TARGARYEN during and after ROBERT 'S REBELLION  when he served in her father 's KINGSGUARD END END BEGIN BEGIN BARRISTAN hails her as the rightful queen and asks to serve in her queensguard END END

BEGIN BEGIN JON SNOW marches slowly SOUTH with the FREE FOLK ARMY of king BEYOND the WALL MANCE RAYDER END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE explains that his ARMY is a diverse force  formed of about ninety different groups or clans of WILDLINGS  who speak SEVEN different languages  and have numerous internal rivalries END END BEGIN BEGIN however  he managed to unite them all by telling them the truth that they will all DIE if they remain NORTH of the WALL END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE brings JON to one of his scouts  ORELL END END BEGIN BEGIN he is sitting silently with his eyes rolled back as an eagle circles above him END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE says that he is a warg  and YGRITTE is surprised that JON doesn 't know what that is END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE explains that a warg is a person who is capable of entering the mind of an animal  seeing what it sees and even controlling its actions END END BEGIN BEGIN ORELL controls his menagerie to scout miles ahead END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE asks him what he has seen  and ORELL says he saw the FIST of the FIRST MEN and many DEAD crows  END END

BEGIN BEGIN when they are on the move again  JOJEN and BRAN discuss his WOLF dreams END END BEGIN BEGIN JOJEN explains that BRAN himself is a warg END END BEGIN BEGIN JOJEN says that it starts out as vivid dreams seeing the world through his WOLF 'S eyes  but with practice he will be able to consciously enter the mind of his WOLF and control its actions END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN asks if prophetic dreams are part of being a warg  but JOJEN explains that 's a different  related ability END END BEGIN BEGIN the SIGHT allows those who possess it to see events that haven 't happened yet  or events that happened LONG before they were born  or events happening now but thousands of miles away END END BEGIN BEGIN JOJEN confirms that BRAN 'S dream of his father EDDARD the day he died was an example of the SIGHT  and that JOJEN himself had a similar dream the same day END END BEGIN BEGIN he says that when he told his father  lord HOWLAND REED  he openly wept  for he correctly realized that his son 's dream signified that EDDARD was DEAD END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN says that HOWLAND was a GREAT friend of his father EDDARD 'S who fought alongside him during ROBERT 'S REBELLION END END BEGIN BEGIN JOJEN says that HOWLAND doesn 't like to talk about the war much END END BEGIN BEGIN JOJEN confirms that BRAN wasn 't simply experiencing a vision of JOJEN in his earlier dream  but that he reached out with his mind to contact BRAN in his dream  and that he REMEMBERS seeing the THREE EYED RAVEN too END END

BEGIN BEGIN  DARK WINGS  DARK WORDS is the SECOND EPISODE of the third SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the twenty SECOND EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on APRIL 7  2013 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by co executive producer vanessa taylor and directed by daniel minahan END END 
BEGIN BEGIN SANSA STARK is introduced to OLENNA TYRELL and is incautious when questioned about king JOFFREY BARATHEON END END BEGIN BEGIN SHAE asks TYRION LANNISTER for help protecting SANSA END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME LANNISTER provokes BRIENNE into a duel but finds himself recaptured END END BEGIN BEGIN ARYA STARK crosses paths with the BROTHERHOOD WITHOUT BANNERS and is recognized by their NEW prisoner SANDOR CLEGANE END END BEGIN BEGIN RAVENS bring DARK NEWS to the king in the NORTH at HARRENHAL his BROTHERS are still missing and HOSTER TULLY has died END END BEGIN BEGIN JON SNOW learns about wargs from the FREE FOLK END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN STARK is surprised to meet NEW allies in the barren NORTH END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in ASTAPOR  DAENERYS  accompanied by ser JORAH MORMONT and ser BARRISTAN SELMY  WALKS along a SEA WALL known as the WALK of PUNISHMENT END END BEGIN BEGIN here  any slave who showed insubordination of any type is strapped to a cross and left to DIE out in public  as a warning to all other slaves END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS offers a condemned MAN WATER  but he refuses to drink  saying he just wants to DIE quickly END END 
BEGIN BEGIN JORAH and BARRISTAN continue to disagree on whether or not DAENERYS should purchase the UNSULLIED END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH insists that it is their only chance to get an ARMY  but BARRISTAN believes this is not the honorable way  as slavery is illegal and abhorred in the SEVEN KINGDOMS END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH claims that not only will the slave soldiers be treated better in her service  but innocent people will also be spared in war because the UNSULLIED only do as they are ordered END END BEGIN BEGIN they have no human or masculine urges in their bodies  and therefore will not KILL civilians or rape innocent women  unlike most male soldiers who would succumb to those urges in the heat of BATTLE END END BEGIN BEGIN BARRISTAN retorts that when her older brother RHAEGAR led his ARMY in the BATTLE of the TRIDENT  MEN fought and died for RHAEGAR because they believed in him  because they loved him not because they were slave soldiers whose FREE will had been stripped away END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH responds that RHAEGAR indeed fought honorably and nobly  but that in the END RHAEGAR died END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS was born months after ROBERT BARATHEON killed RHAEGAR at the BATTLE of the TRIDENT  and only knew her cruel and half MAD brother VISERYS  so she asks ser BARRISTAN if he knew RHAEGAR END END BEGIN BEGIN SELMY was a member of the TARGARYEN KINGSGUARD and thus knew RHAEGAR well he fought beside him and bled beside him at the TRIDENT END END BEGIN BEGIN BARRISTAN says that RHAEGAR was the finest MAN he ever met  the LAST dragon END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS grows quiet and says she wishes she 'd known her older brother  but that RHAEGAR was not the LAST dragon she is  END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS speaks with KRAZNYS mo nakloz  as he shows her his slave soldiers  the UNSULLIED END END BEGIN BEGIN he repeatedly insults and mocks DAENERYS in his native tongue  leaving his slave translator MISSANDEI of naath to clean up his crude and very insulting WORDS into more respectful language END END BEGIN BEGIN at one point  she pauses  wondering how to twist a particularly coarse insult from KRAZNYS  and DAENERYS notices her reluctance to directly translate END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS says she will take all 8  000 UNSULLIED soldiers  including those in training END END BEGIN BEGIN KRAZNYS laughs and retorts that she can barely afford 100 UNSULLIED END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS surprises him by telling him she has DRAGONS  and is willing to trade one END END BEGIN BEGIN this offer stops KRAZNYS in his tracks  yet DAENERYS repeatedly affirms that he MAY only have one of her DRAGONS END END BEGIN BEGIN they strike a deal that she MAY have all the UNSULLIED soldiers in exchange for her biggest dragon END END BEGIN BEGIN both JORAH and SELMY strongly object  and plead to DAENERYS that while soldiers are valuable  it is DRAGONS that will ultimately WIN her the IRON THRONE END END BEGIN BEGIN she ignores them  and concludes the deal with KRAZNYS  and also demands MISSANDEI as a token of FAITH END END BEGIN BEGIN upon leaving the room  she scolds JORAH and SELMY  telling them that while she values their advice  they should NEVER again question her in public END END

BEGIN BEGIN at some point  before or after this event  SANDOR CLEGANE and ARYA STARK arrive at the bloody GATE of the EYRIE and are informed of LYSA 'S death by ser donnel WAYNWOOD END END BEGIN BEGIN the HOUND stares in shock  while ARYA begins laughing due to the irony END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in the LAST hours before his trial by combat  TYRION and JAIME share a final drink in TYRION 'S cell and reminisce about ORSON LANNISTER  their simple minded cousin who spent his days smashing beetles with a ROCK END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION tells JAIME of how he used to observe ORSON day after day in an attempt to understand his motives  but in the END he was NEVER able to COME to reach any understanding END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION asks JAIME if he thinks OBERYN stands a chance  but JAIME is not optimistic END END BEGIN BEGIN as a bell rings out to announce daybreak in the CITY  JAIME takes his leave  wishing his brother luck END END 
BEGIN BEGIN LANNISTER guardsmen escort TYRION to the arena  where a large crowd has assembled END END BEGIN BEGIN he grows apprehensive to find a helm less OBERYN drinking  and wearing very LIGHT armor in comparison to his opponent  ser GREGOR CLEGANE  clad from head to foot in heavy armor and wielding a greatsword END END BEGIN BEGIN OBERYN dismisses TYRION 'S concerns  noting that he always drinks before a fight and favors speed over protection END END BEGIN BEGIN as GREGOR and his squire make their way to the arena  ELLARIA becomes concerned  noting that the MOUNTAIN is the biggest MAN she 's ever seen  but OBERYN remains confident that he will emerge triumphant END END BEGIN BEGIN GRAND maester PYCELLE steps into the arena and begins making a LONG winded speech asking the GODS to favor the innocent before TYWIN LANNISTER cuts him short and begins the trial by combat END END

BEGIN BEGIN however  OBERYN stands too close to his seemingly defeated opponent  and GREGOR manages to trip and seize him END END BEGIN BEGIN berserk with fury  GREGOR grabs OBERYN by the throat and lifts him off the ground  smashing out most of his teeth with a single devastating punch END END BEGIN BEGIN climbing on top of OBERYN  GREGOR finally admits for all to hear that he raped and killed ELIA as he gouges out OBERYN 'S eyes with his thumbs before crushing the VIPER 'S skull between his HANDS  which he proclaims having done the same to his sister END END BEGIN BEGIN as ELLARIA screams in horror  a stunned silence sweeps over the crowd END END BEGIN BEGIN the short joyful moments for TYRION and JAIME are shattered  as TYWIN stands and proclaims the will of the GODS is clear TYRION is guilty and sentenced to death END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION cannot even reply  shockingly staring in catatonic astonishment at OBERYN 'S skull crushed corpse  as does JAIME the only different reaction is from CERSEI  who stares at OBERYN 'S slaughtered body  listening to TYRION 'S death sentence while smirking in vindication END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  the MOUNTAIN and the VIPER is the eighth EPISODE of the fourth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES 1  END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the thirty eighth EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on june 1  2014 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by producers DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS and directed by alex graves END END 
BEGIN BEGIN unexpected visitors arrive in MOLE 'S TOWN END END BEGIN BEGIN LITTLEFINGER 'S motives are questioned END END BEGIN BEGIN RAMSAY tries to prove himself to his father END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION 'S fate is decided END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  JON and SAM are standing WATCH atop the WALL  staring out into the darkness of the NORTH and awaiting the imminent wildling invasion END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM attempts to interrogate JON about what it was like to be with a WOMAN  stating that as their deaths are likely imminent  it MAY be his LAST chance to find out END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM brings up that the vows of the NIGHT 'S WATCH only explicitly forbid members from taking wives or producing CHILDREN  and that other activities are open to interpretation END END BEGIN BEGIN JON replies glumly that ALLISER THORNE most likely does not care about their interpretations END END BEGIN BEGIN when further pressed by SAM to describe lying down with YGRITTE  JON attempts to explain but is unable to properly express it  proclaiming exasperatedly that he 's not a bleeding poet END END

BEGIN BEGIN  maester AEMON finds SAM in the CASTLE BLACK library END END BEGIN BEGIN meanwhile  SAM is caught reading a BOOK about WILDLINGS by maester AEMON END END BEGIN BEGIN AEMON correctly guesses that SAM is reading the BOOK because he wants to know what kind of fate might have befallen GILLY if she fell into wildling HANDS during the SACK of MOLE 'S TOWN END END BEGIN BEGIN he also surmises that SAM has shown such a keen interest in her fate because he is in love with her  despite SAM 'S protests to the contrary END END BEGIN BEGIN AEMON muses about the girl he once loved  stating that he can still picture her as clear as day and that she is more real than SAM is END END BEGIN BEGIN after being dismissed by AEMON  SAM leaves the maester 's chambers only to hear GILLY at the GATE begging to be allowed inside  revealing her survival of the MOLE 'S TOWN massacre and her identity as the cloaked figure approaching CASTLE BLACK END END BEGIN BEGIN PYPAR attempts to deny her passage into the CASTLE  saying he is not allowed to open the GATE under any circumstances END END BEGIN BEGIN however  SAM roars at PYP to allow her in  causing PYP to relent and let her in END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM promises GILLY wherever she goes next he will go too  but their reunion is cut short by TWO blows from the horn  indicating that MANCE 'S wildling ARMY has finally begun their assault END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM rushes to get GILLY safely inside the CASTLE while other BROTHERS of the NIGHT 'S WATCH prepare for the imminent attack by WILDLINGS END END 
BEGIN BEGIN on top of the WALL  JON hears the horn blowing and looks NORTH  witnessing a tremendous conflagration to the NORTH  just as MANCE had promised END END BEGIN BEGIN SOUTH of the WALL  the THENN warg 's owl also spots the FIRE and informs STYR and TORMUND that the time has COME to attack CASTLE BLACK END END BEGIN BEGIN JON approaches ser ALLISER THORNE  who finally relents and admits that they should have heeded JON 'S advice and blocked the GATES END END BEGIN BEGIN he grimly muses that leadership often means being SECOND guessed by every clever little twat with a mouth and when a MAN in charge SECOND guesses himself  all is doomed END END BEGIN BEGIN steeling himself for the impending SIEGE  THORNE begins barking orders to the archers  preparing them to FIRE upon the attackers massing below END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  SAM and GILLY share a kiss END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM brings GILLY and her baby to a storage room where she can hide END END BEGIN BEGIN GILLY wants SAM to stay with her as he promised  but he cannot as he swore to defend the WALL as a brother of the NIGHT 'S WATCH END END BEGIN BEGIN before he leaves her  GILLY begs SAM to promise her that he won 't DIE and the TWO finally share a kiss END END BEGIN BEGIN as SAM and PYPAR are preparing arrows at the southern GATE  PYPAR laments that he has NEVER seen a real BATTLE before or ever even held an edged blade END END BEGIN BEGIN PYPAR asks how SAM is not afraid  but SAM replies that he is  as there are thousands of WILDLINGS about to overrun them END END BEGIN BEGIN PYPAR asks how he managed to KILL a WHITE WALKER while being afraid  and SAM says that at that moment  he just had to do something or GILLY would have been killed and her baby would have been taken END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM further explains that at that moment  he wasn 't himself he was nothing  and when you are nothing there is nothing to be afraid of END END BEGIN BEGIN however  he explains the reason he is afraid now is because i 'm not nothing anymore END END 
BEGIN BEGIN meanwhile  YGRITTE spies on the CASTLE to scout numbers of defenders END END BEGIN BEGIN she tells the other WILDLINGS that most of the guards are at the top of the WALL and that few are left in the CASTLE END END BEGIN BEGIN the group immediately take off towards CASTLE BLACK 'S southern GATE  while YGRITTE seems to have SECOND thoughts END END BEGIN BEGIN NORTH of the WALL  the massive wildling ARMY emerges from the WOODS  their numbers including giants riding atop mammoths END END BEGIN BEGIN ALLISER orders the archers on the WALL to nock their arrows  but they draw instead while GRENN accidentally drops a barrel down the WALL END END BEGIN BEGIN ALLISER angrily drills his MEN on properly following orders when another horn blows from down below at CASTLE BLACK  signalling the unanticipated appearance of TORMUND 'S band of WILDLINGS at the CASTLE 'S southern entrance END END BEGIN BEGIN realizing the dire need for experienced MEN to defend the KEEP from the surprise attack  ALLISER orders JANOS SLYNT to assume command of the WALL 'S defenses and heads below to join the melee END END 
BEGIN BEGIN below  TORMUND and STYR 'S forces charge the GATE while YGRITTE  acting as a sniper  manages to pick off SEVERAL MEN defending the GATE with her bow END END BEGIN BEGIN PYPAR is firing a crossbow as SAM assists by reloading another crossbow  but PYPAR 'S aim is poor due to inexperience and nerves and he repeatedly misses his shots END END BEGIN BEGIN the band of WILDLINGS manage to reach CASTLE BLACK 'S WALLS and begin scaling them using grappling hooks and ropes  forcing SAM and PYP to retreat END END

BEGIN BEGIN  the WATCHERS on the WALL is the ninth EPISODE of the fourth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES 1  END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the thirty ninth EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on june 8  2014 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by producers DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS and directed by neil marshall END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the NIGHT 'S WATCH  although hopelessly outnumbered  attempts to defend CASTLE BLACK from MANCE RAYDER 'S massive wildling ARMY  who plan to SIEGE the fortress from the NORTH END END BEGIN BEGIN meanwhile  a secret garrison of WILDLINGS including TORMUND  STYR  and YGRITTE are poised to launch a surprise attack from the SOUTH of the WALL END END 
BEGIN BEGIN JON SNOW emerges from the outer GATE of the WALL and begins trudging NORTH through the aftermath of the previous NIGHT 'S BATTLE towards MANCE RAYDER 'S war camp END END BEGIN BEGIN JON eventually reaches the tree line and is quickly surrounded by WILDLINGS  who bring him before MANCE  who notes that he is wearing the BLACK of the NIGHT 'S WATCH again END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE brings JON inside his tent  and questions his status as a traitor END END BEGIN BEGIN JON confesses that his time spent with the WILDLINGS was all part of a plan orchestrated by QHORIN HALFHAND to get JON to infiltrate MANCE 'S ARMY  and that QHORIN tricked MANCE into trusting JON by allowing JON to KILL QHORIN himself in a fight END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE asks about YGRITTE and JON reveals that she died at the BATTLE of CASTLE BLACK  though not by his HANDS END END BEGIN BEGIN saddened  MANCE proposes that they drink a toast to her memory  but JON is hesitant when given an unfamiliar drink END END BEGIN BEGIN JON accepts after MANCE assures him that if he 'd wanted to KILL JON  poison would be the LAST of his methods END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE then asks about the giant who got through the GATE but NEVER came out  and JON informs MANCE that the giant perished attempting to breach the inner GATE at the HANDS of his friend GRENN END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE ruefully notes that the giant was named MAG the mighty  and he was king of the giants  the LAST of a bloodline stretching back thousands of years before the FIRST MEN entered WESTEROS  to which JON then glibly notes that his friend GRENN was from a farm END END BEGIN BEGIN they have another toast to MAG and GRENN END END 
BEGIN BEGIN JON then proposes his terms to MANCE mance is to turn his ARMY around and return HOME END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE immediately counters that the NIGHT 'S WATCH is low on oil  arrows  and MEN  and when he sent his full force against the WALL the NIGHT 'S WATCH threw everything they had at him to repel the attack END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE guesses there are no more than 50 MEN left guarding CASTLE BLACK  but JON lies and insists that there are still over 1  000 MEN defending the garrison END END BEGIN BEGIN however  MANCE calls JON 'S bluff and reveals that after seeing how few MEN were defending CASTLE BLACK  he sent 400 MEN about FIVE miles west to CLIMB an unmanned section of the WALL  and they will attack CASTLE BLACK 'S weak southern side as soon as he gives the order END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE then changes his demeanor and reveals that his people have suffered enough bloodshed and that he has no intention of conquering the LANDS SOUTH of the WALL that the WILDLINGS are moving SOUTH to seek refuge from the growing threat of the WHITE WALKERS just as those SOUTH of the WALL are END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE then makes his counteroffer if the NIGHT 'S WATCH will open the GATES to the WILDLINGS and allow them to pass through the WALL  no more harm will COME to the BLACK BROTHERS END END BEGIN BEGIN however  if his terms are refused  his wildling ARMY will slaughter every LAST member of the NIGHT 'S WATCH and move SOUTH by force END END 
BEGIN BEGIN MANCE then notices that JON is eyeing a cooking knife  and quickly deduces that JON came to parley with MANCE simply so he could assassinate him END END BEGIN BEGIN he notes that at that moment his personal guards are far enough across the room that JON might actually be able to KILL him before being cut down himself  but that JON must have known he would DIE assassinating MANCE END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE is shocked and questions JON if this is what the NIGHT 'S WATCH has sunk to killing a MAN who let him into his own tent  accepting a parley in good FAITH  who shared food and drink with him  and who even offered him relatively reasonable peace terms END END BEGIN BEGIN JON hesitates  but before anyone can make a move  war horns are heard from OUTSIDE END END BEGIN BEGIN MANCE 'S guards safely grab JON during the distraction  and MANCE demands to know if the NIGHT 'S WATCH is attacking them  but JON admits that it 's just as MANCE said the NIGHT 'S WATCH doesn 't have remotely enough numbers to leave the safety of the WALL and attack END END 
BEGIN BEGIN columns of heavy horse carrying hundreds of mounted cavalry charge into the wildling camp carrying the flaming stag BANNERS of HOUSE BARATHEON of DRAGONSTONE  and are led by none other than STANNIS BARATHEON and DAVOS seaworth END END BEGIN BEGIN the WILDLINGS are caught in their own camp  resting from the BATTLE the NIGHT before and only expecting attacks from the WALL  so their eastern flank is completely undefended END END BEGIN BEGIN as they are undisciplined and have no experience fighting heavily armored cavalry  they are quickly dispatched by STANNIS ' riders  who attack the wildling camp from both sides in TWO separate columns that catch the WILDLINGS in a perfect double envelopment END END BEGIN BEGIN quickly cutting the wildling forces down  STANNIS and DAVOS ride up to MANCE  who throws down his weapons in surrender  officially ending the WILDLINGS ' SIEGE of CASTLE BLACK END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAVOS introduces STANNIS as the true king of the SEVEN KINGDOMS  but MANCE wryly points out that they are not currently in the SEVEN KINGDOMS END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS demands that it is customary to kneel when surrendering to a king END END BEGIN BEGIN resignedly  MANCE says that the FREE FOLK do not kneel  knowing that STANNIS will KILL him if he does not END END BEGIN BEGIN DAVOS  however  asks what a MAN of the NIGHT 'S WATCH is doing in the camp  and JON explains that he came to treaty with the king BEYOND the WALL END END BEGIN BEGIN JON says that he knows that STANNIS is the true king  as his own father died supporting his claim  revealing himself as the bastard son of EDDARD STARK END END BEGIN BEGIN this makes STANNIS regard JON more seriously END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS proclaims that EDDARD was an honorable MAN  and asks JON what NED would have done with MANCE END END BEGIN BEGIN JON responds that MANCE could have killed him or tortured him when he was his captive but instead he spared his life  so instead of killing MANCE he should be taken prisoner and interrogated END END BEGIN BEGIN before they leave the wildling camp  JON also urges STANNIS to burn the DEAD before nightfall END END BEGIN BEGIN  END END 
BEGIN BEGIN back at CASTLE BLACK  a funeral is held for the slain members of the NIGHT 'S WATCH  who have been arranged in a huge funeral pyre in the CASTLE courtyard END END BEGIN BEGIN maester AEMON delivers a eulogy  saying that they died to protect the MEN  women  and CHILDREN of the SOUTH who will NEVER even know who they were  that it is the duty of the surviving BLACK BROTHERS to KEEP alive their memory END END BEGIN BEGIN AEMON closes his speech with the customary line  and now their WATCH has ENDED  which is repeated by the gathered MEN END END BEGIN BEGIN SAMWELL then aids AEMON in setting the pyre alight  which is continued by JON and other MEN carrying torches END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS and DAVOS look on  along with queen SELYSE and princess SHIREEN END END BEGIN BEGIN JON looks across the flames and catches the gaze of MELISANDRE  who is standing on the opposite side of the pyre END END BEGIN BEGIN MELISANDRE seems intrigued  her piercing stare clearly making JON uneasy END END 
BEGIN BEGIN AFTERWARDS  JON enters the chamber of the CASTLE where TORMUND is being held END END BEGIN BEGIN TORMUND asks why blind OLD maester AEMON patched up his arrow wounds  and JON says that AEMON is sworn to heal all wounded MEN  friend or foe END END BEGIN BEGIN TORMUND asks if JON really loved YGRITTE END END BEGIN BEGIN JON doesn 't respond END END BEGIN BEGIN TORMUND says that YGRITTE truly loved him  and that he knew because although she NEVER admitted it  she talked only of killing him  revealing her true feelings for him if she hadn 't loved him  she wouldn 't have been so angered by his betrayal  END END BEGIN BEGIN saddened  TORMUND implores JON that YGRITTE 'S final resting place should be in the real NORTH END END BEGIN BEGIN JON then takes YGRITTE 'S corpse to the NORTH side of the WALL and builds a funeral pyre for her near a sacred heart tree END END BEGIN BEGIN JON looks at his lover one LAST time and LIGHTS her pyre  and weeps silently as he turns his back and heads HOME END END 
BEGIN BEGIN far to the NORTH  BRAN STARK and the REED CHILDREN continue their journey to find the THREE EYED RAVEN  though they are on the brink of exhaustion END END BEGIN BEGIN JOJEN REED has grown sick and and he is barely able to stand  eventually collapsing into the SNOW END END BEGIN BEGIN as MEERA begs JOJEN to gather what little strength he can muster to continue forward  BRAN calls out to them  revealing that they have found the massive heart tree that BRAN has seen in his visions END END BEGIN BEGIN as they approach the tree  wights burst up from the SNOW  grabbing JOJEN 'S ankles and attempting to drag him under the ICE END END BEGIN BEGIN these wights appear far older than those seen near the WALL  appearing as ghastly skeletal warriors who move with surprising agility END END BEGIN BEGIN MEERA attempts to defend JOJEN from the wights  but they begin to swarm over HODOR  who is too scared to fight back END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN wargs into HODOR 'S mind and begins fighting off the wights with the aid of his direwolf SUMMER  but more wights KEEP bursting through the ICE and they are quickly overwhelmed END END

BEGIN BEGIN in MEEREEN  queen DAENERYS TARGARYEN sits in her THRONE room where she is receiving the day 's supplicants END END BEGIN BEGIN an OLD MAN named FENNESZ approaches the THRONE  FIRST speaking in HIGH VALYRIAN but then revealing that he also knows the common tongue END END BEGIN BEGIN FENNESZ explains that he was not one of the slaves who toiled away at manual labor  but a well educated teacher and servant to master MIGHDAL  who employed him as a teacher for his own CHILDREN END END BEGIN BEGIN he tells daenarys that master MIGHDAL 'S SEVEN year OLD daughter calla admires DAENERYS  having learned of the TARGARYEN dynasty through FENNESZ 'S teachings END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as a servant of master MIGHDAL  FENNESZ was well treated and even well respected in the household  but when DAENERYS forcibly freed all of the slaves in the CITY she did not understand the full scale complications of suddenly having to care for so many people END END BEGIN BEGIN FENNESZ originally stayed in master MIGHDAL 'S HOUSE after she took the CITY  and MIGHDAL 'S CHILDREN begged him to stay  but MIGHDAL and FENNESZ agreed that he must leave rather than face reprisals  forcing FENNESZ to become homeless END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS insists that she had established mess HALLS to feed the freed slaves and barracks to HOUSE them END END BEGIN BEGIN fennez says that he has visited these refugee centers and they are not very safe the young prey on the OLD  assaulting and robbing them END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS insists that her UNSULLIED will restore order  but FENNESZ points out that even assuming that they are able to ensure his physical safety  he has lost his livelihood and his purpose and is too OLD to start anew END END BEGIN BEGIN therefore  he has COME to DAENERYS to beg her permission to sell himself back to MIGHDAL END END BEGIN BEGIN she is shocked that he would want to be owned as a slave again  as a MAN might own a goat or a chair END END BEGIN BEGIN he implores her that the young MAY rejoice in her NEW world  but for those too OLD to change  there is only fear and squalor END END BEGIN BEGIN nor  he says  is he alone there are many supplicants waiting OUTSIDE lining up to make similar requests END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS is crestfallen  and says she did not liberate the slaves of MEEREEN only to preside over the very injustice she sought to destroy  but surprisingly relents and admits that freedom means making one 's own choices END END BEGIN BEGIN therefore she will allow FENNESZ to enter into a labor contract with MIGHDAL  but lasting no more than one year END END BEGIN BEGIN he earnestly thanks her  and leaves END END BEGIN BEGIN ser BARRISTAN SELMY warns DAENERYS that the MASTERS will assuredly take advantage of this  quickly making contracts with all of the displaced former slaves until they are all slaves again in all but NAME END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the next supplicant then enters  a shepherd carrying a bundle in his arms  similarly to the herdsman who came to show the BONES of their livestock which DAENERYS 'S DRAGONS burned in order to be reimbursed END END BEGIN BEGIN the shepherd timidly approaches and states that he is unable to speak in the common tongue and requires MISSANDEI to translate END END BEGIN BEGIN distraught  he tells daenarys that the winged SHADOW came  placing the bundle on the ground and opening it to reveal charred BONES of a human child END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS 'S largest dragon the BLACK one  DROGON has roasted the MAN 'S THREE year OLD daughter zalla until this is all that was left of her END END BEGIN BEGIN horrified  DAENERYS meets with MISSANDEI and GREY WORM in private to discuss how to deal with the growing threat the DRAGONS are posing to the people of MEEREEN END END BEGIN BEGIN GREY WORM reports that DROGON was LAST seen flying over the BLACK cliffs THREE days ago  but he can no longer be found END END BEGIN BEGIN realizing that she can no longer control her DRAGONS  DAENERYS tells them to head with her to the catacombs under the CITY END END BEGIN BEGIN later  she leads her remaining TWO DRAGONS  RHAEGAL and viserion  into the catacombs  where they are distracted by sheep carcasses END END BEGIN BEGIN as they are feeding  DAENERYS personally locks huge IRON collars around their NECKS  which are secured by heavy CHAINS END END BEGIN BEGIN she weeps as she does so  as it is symbolically reducing her remaining CHILDREN to chained up slaves themselves END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS wordlessly leaves and closes the huge STONE DOOR to the catacombs behind her as her DRAGONS grow distressed and pathetically call after her when they attempt to follow and realize they are chained in place END END

BEGIN BEGIN  the CHILDREN is the tenth and final EPISODE of the fourth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES 1  END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the fortieth EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it aired on june 15  2014 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by producers DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS and directed by alex graves END END
