BEGIN BEGIN  HIGH SPARROW is the third EPISODE of the fifth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the forty third EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on APRIL 26  2015 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS  and directed by mark mylod END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in BRAAVOS  ARYA sees the many faced GOD END END BEGIN BEGIN in king 's LANDING  queen MARGAERY enjoys her NEW husband END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION and VARYS WALK the LONG BRIDGE of VOLANTIS END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at a SMALL COUNCIL meeting  master of coin MACE TYRELL brings bad NEWS that the IRON BANK of BRAAVOS is starting to call in its debts from WESTEROS END END BEGIN BEGIN they have started by calling in a tenth of the IRON THRONE 'S current debts to the BANK  which it can only afford half of as rebuilding the royal fleet was also a massive expense END END BEGIN BEGIN MACE offers that HOUSE TYRELL could front the money for the time being  but CERSEI clearly does not want to give the TYRELLS more power over the CROWN END END BEGIN BEGIN instead  she says that they will send MACE himself to BRAAVOS to negotiate for more time  because sending such a HIGH ranking official will show the BANK how seriously they take their large debts END END BEGIN BEGIN MACE is oblivious that this is also CERSEI 'S way of removing him from the capital  and takes it as a HIGH HONOR as well as that CERSEI will send ser MERYN TRANT of the KINGSGUARD along to guard him END END BEGIN BEGIN after he leaves  PYCELLE bitterly points out that the SMALL COUNCIL is growing even smaller the only THREE members left in the capital are PYCELLE  CERSEI  and her lackey QYBURN  but she says it hasn 't quite grown SMALL enough yet END END 
BEGIN BEGIN CERSEI then meets with the HIGH SPARROW  who by her influence  has been elected as the NEW HIGH SEPTON of the FAITH of the SEVEN END END BEGIN BEGIN CERSEI is trying to build up a NEW alliance between the CROWN and the FAITH  as a counterweight against the large political influence the TYRELLS now possess END END BEGIN BEGIN CERSEI points out to the HIGH SPARROW that the war of the FIVE KINGS has devastated much of the countryside  resulting in SEPTS being burned  clergymen attacked  and even SILENT SISTERS raped END END BEGIN BEGIN bodies of holy MEN are piling up in the streets END END BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SPARROW admits that WARS make MEN obey the sword more than the GODS END END BEGIN BEGIN CERSEI points out that before the TARGARYENS  the military order known as the FAITH MILITANT dispensed the justice of the SEVEN END END BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SEPTON is confused  as the TARGARYENS disbanded the FAITH MILITANT over TWO centuries ago END END BEGIN BEGIN CERSEI explains that  as part of the NEW alliance she hopes to build between the CROWN and the FAITH  she will tell her son to repeal the law and allow the FAITH MILITANT to be reestablished and re armed an ARMY whose purpose is to defend the FAITH  holy MEN  and the smallfolk and which will incidentally be turned against the CROWN 'S enemies END END BEGIN BEGIN she then advises him that there is a GREAT sinner in their midst who has been shielded by gold and power END END BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SPARROW replies with a wish for the father to judge him justly END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the NEW FAITH MILITANT STORM the streets of king 's LANDING  attacking taverns  brothels  and street vendors selling idols from other religions END END BEGIN BEGIN the CITY WATCH look on  helpless  and do not intervene END END BEGIN BEGIN they ransack LITTLEFINGER 'S brothel  dragging prostitutes like marei out into the street by their hair END END BEGIN BEGIN OLYVAR is struck and ignored as they barge in he then sees that in another room they have singled out a MAN having sex with one of the male prostitutes  and approach him with a knife END END BEGIN BEGIN OLYVAR flees END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  TOMMEN attempts to have his brother in law LORAS released  but fails END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as a sign of their zealotry  the FAITH MILITANT have the SEVEN pointed star symbol of the FAITH carved into their foreheads including LANCEL  who leads a squad of the FAITH MILITANT to apprehend LORAS TYRELL while he is sparring in the practice yard END END BEGIN BEGIN LANCEL proclaims that LORAS ' sexual perversions are sins against the LAWS of GODS and MEN  and LORAS is dragged off END END BEGIN BEGIN MARGAERY TYRELL is furious at TOMMEN for her brother 's arrest  then tries to manipulate him by weeping at how hurt she is that he let this happen to LORAS END END BEGIN BEGIN TOMMEN then goes to his MOTHER and  briefly standing up to her  demands that LORAS be released at once END END BEGIN BEGIN CERSEI calmly points out that she didn 't arrest LORAS  the FAITH MILITANT simply dragged him off and imprisoned him  so he should ask the HIGH SPARROW to release him END END BEGIN BEGIN TOMMEN naively thinks the HIGH SPARROW will simply do as he requests  so he heads to the GREAT SEPT of BAELOR with FIVE KINGSGUARD and SEVERAL LANNISTER guards END END BEGIN BEGIN the path to the GREAT SEPT is blocked by the FAITH MILITANT  who say that the HIGH SPARROW is praying and does not wish to be disturbed END END BEGIN BEGIN the KINGSGUARD request that TOMMEN let them KILL the FAITH MILITANT to pass END END BEGIN BEGIN TOMMEN is surprised at this and does not want to risk bloodshed escalating matters particularly  shedding BLOOD on holy ground END END BEGIN BEGIN unsure of what to do  the mob of commoners behind him starts shouting that he is really a bastard and an abomination of incest END END BEGIN BEGIN realizing this is not going to END well  TOMMEN meekly withdraws back to the RED KEEP END END BEGIN BEGIN MARGAERY is even more upset at how ineffectual young TOMMEN was  so she leaves saying that she is going to bring her grandmother OLENNA back to the capital to deal with this END END 
BEGIN BEGIN JAIME LANNISTER and ser BRONN are on a PENTOSHI merchant ship  which is headed to OLDTOWN in the reach END END BEGIN BEGIN they sail past TARTH  off the coast of the STORMLANDS  which JAIME mistakenly identifies as estermont END END BEGIN BEGIN the captain corrects him  stating that they are sailing through the sapphire isle  which reminds him of BRIENNE END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME explains to BRONN that he bribed the captain to let them take a SMALL boat to shore as they pass DORNE  and they will land just OUTSIDE of SUNSPEAR and the adjacent WATER GARDENS END END BEGIN BEGIN below decks  BRONN remarks on why JAIME must want to go and protect princess MYRCELLA for himself he 's the one who let TYRION escape  and he hopes this will make up for that END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME curtly says that VARYS did when in fact  JAIME forced VARYS to help him FREE TYRION  END END BEGIN BEGIN BRONN says that if JAIME ever sees TYRION again JAIME should give him his regards JAIME angrily says that if he sees his brother again  he 's going to split him in TWO for murdering their father TYWIN END END 
BEGIN BEGIN BRONN rows the pair ashore at dusk  though JAIME can 't help row with his one HAND END END BEGIN BEGIN when they awake the next morning BRONN KILLS a snake that was near JAIME 'S head and roasts it up for breakfast END END BEGIN BEGIN BRONN is worried that the ship 's captain will subsequently spread word that a LANNISTER is in DORNE JAIME says he bribed him with a large bag of gold  but BRONN still worries END END BEGIN BEGIN a mounted patrol soon COMES by  however  and sees their tracks in the SAND END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME and BRONN present themselves and try to pass off that they are simple travelers and their boat capsized in the NIGHT  but the ruse doesn 't work  and the sentries demand that they drop their weapons so they can be taken prisoner and their identities confirmed END END BEGIN BEGIN BRONN plants his sword in the SAND then quickly throws his dagger in the lead sentry 's throat END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME and BRONN draw their SWORDS and fight the rest END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME can 't fight very well left handed so BRONN KILLS one sentry 's horse in order for JAIME to fight him on foot END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME is being overpowered but catches the sentry 's sword with his metal HAND at the LAST moment END END BEGIN BEGIN he then uses the distraction to land a killing blow to the sentry with his left HAND END END BEGIN BEGIN BRONN  having finished off the other sentries  notes that they now have their horses fine DORNISH SAND steeds  capable of running a day and a NIGHT WITHOUT tiring END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME says the bodies need to be buried so they won 't raise more questions END END BEGIN BEGIN BRONN says it will take a lot of time to dig holes for them all  though JAIME again points out that he can 't really do much digging with one HAND END END BEGIN BEGIN annoyed  BRONN then drags off the bodies to bury END END 
BEGIN BEGIN meanwhile  elsewhere OUTSIDE of SUNSPEAR  ELLARIA SAND meets with THREE of the eight SAND SNAKES  her lover OBERYN MARTELL 'S bastard daughters END END BEGIN BEGIN OBARA SAND  the eldest  is the daughter of a peasant NYMERIA SAND commonly called NYM is the daughter of an eastern noblewoman the youngest of the THREE  TYENE SAND  is ELLARIA 'S own daughter END END BEGIN BEGIN she informs them that PRINCE DORAN MARTELL will not raise DORNE 'S armies to avenge his brother 's death END END BEGIN BEGIN they worry that they have no ARMY to march against the LANNISTERS  but ELLARIA tells them that they don 't need one to start a war  all they need to do is KILL CERSEI 'S daughter MYRCELLA  currently in DORAN 'S possession END END 
BEGIN BEGIN OBARA then points out that they MAY have a problem END END BEGIN BEGIN the PENTOSHI ship captain found her in planky TOWN  and as BRONN feared  he indeed tried to sell her information about JAIME LANNISTER 'S arrival in DORNE END END BEGIN BEGIN the SAND SNAKES  however  were insulted that he wanted to be paid for such vital information instead of offering it freely  so they took him prisoner and tortured it out of him END END BEGIN BEGIN NYMERIA uses her whip to knock a bucket over  and reveals underneath that they buried the ship 's captain NECK deep in the SAND  with his head under a bucket full of poisonous scorpions END END BEGIN BEGIN they realize that they are now in a race against time to see who can take MYRCELLA from DORAN FIRST JAIME LANNISTER or themselves END END BEGIN BEGIN ELLARIA asks if the THREE girls are with her  knowing this will bring DORNE into war END END BEGIN BEGIN NYMERIA and TYENE say yes END END BEGIN BEGIN OBARA notes that when she FIRST met OBERYN  he was a MAN whom she had NEVER met who one day appeared  said he was her father  and that he was taking her away from her MOTHER END END BEGIN BEGIN her MOTHER wept  but OBERYN said that  we all must choose our BATTLES and the GODS let us choose our weapons END END BEGIN BEGIN he threw his spear at her feet  pointed to her MOTHER 'S tears  then to his spear  and told her to choose END END BEGIN BEGIN she chose the spear and answers ELLARIA that she is with her  as she chose the path of the spear and war LONG ago END END BEGIN BEGIN she then throws her spear to impale the ship captain 's head END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at VOLANTIS  during the NIGHT  JORAH MORMONT knocks out a fisherman and steals his boat  leaving with his captive TYRION LANNISTER END END BEGIN BEGIN later when they are at SEA  TYRION urges for JORAH to remove his gag END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH will not volunteer any information about himself  but from a few observations such as the BEAR sigil on his armor  TYRION quickly surmises that he must be JORAH MORMONT END END BEGIN BEGIN he admits to TYRION that the queen he is taking him to is not CERSEI but DAENERYS END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION recalls from SMALL COUNCIL meetings that JORAH was spying on DAENERYS for VARYS END END BEGIN BEGIN given that he is half the world away from DAENERYS  he also accurately deduces that she must have found out he was spying on her and had him exiled and therefore  he kidnapped TYRION in the hope that presenting him as a GIFT to DAENERYS will get him back in her favor END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION laughs aloud at his situation  informing JORAH that he was already heading to meet DAENERYS  so this is a WASTE of a kidnapping END END BEGIN BEGIN TYRION also points out that there is no guarantee this will assuage DAENERYS  and it is just as likely she will remain angry at JORAH  and welcome himself as an ally END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH smacks TYRION across the face  quieting him down END END 
BEGIN BEGIN JON SNOW trains recruits in the practice yard of CASTLE BLACK  as STANNIS BARATHEON and his wife SELYSE WATCH  along with their daughter SHIREEN END END BEGIN BEGIN SELYSE is worried that STANNIS wishes JON was his son  because she gave him only stillbirths and weakness  but he says that wasn 't her fault END END BEGIN BEGIN MELISANDRE joins them and appears to quite firmly take STANNIS 'S side  declaring that the lord of LIGHT doesn 't care about SHIREEN 'S greyscale disfigurement  and this doesn 't change the fact that she has her father 's BLOOD END END BEGIN BEGIN when SELYSE departs  MELISANDRE discusses the COMING BATTLE to take WINTERFELL from the BOLTONS END END BEGIN BEGIN she asks if STANNIS intends to leave her behind as he did at the BLACKWATER  but STANNIS assures her he won 't this time END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as the NEW lord commander  JON goes over paperwork with SAMWELL TARLY  letters they have received from minor HOUSES offering up a handful of NEW recruits END END BEGIN BEGIN JON balks when SAMWELL HANDS him a request letter for ROOSE BOLTON  saying he killed his brother ROBB END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM points out that ROOSE BOLTON is now the warden of the NORTH  and he has the most recruits to send them much more than the pittances offered by the other minor HOUSES JON has NEVER even heard of END END BEGIN BEGIN he reminds JON that the NIGHT 'S WATCH has sworn an oath of political neutrality END END BEGIN BEGIN with disgust  JON reluctantly signs the letter to the BOLTONS END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as SAM departs  MELISANDRE enters END END BEGIN BEGIN she entreats him to assist STANNIS in retaking WINTERFELL  pointing out that even if he doesn 't become a STARK  his familiarity with the CASTLE could WIN them the BATTLE END END BEGIN BEGIN she also acknowledges that there is a greater war at stake  and asks JON if he is on the side of life or death  undoing her dress and straddling him as she does so END END BEGIN BEGIN she encourages SNOW to take her  as the lord of LIGHT made humans male and female for a reason although clearly tempted  JON refuses  citing his vows  and the fact that STANNIS wouldn 't approve to which MELISANDRE suggests they not tell him  END END BEGIN BEGIN when MELISANDRE points out that he broke his vows once before  SNOW acknowledges that he still feels for his deceased love END END BEGIN BEGIN MELISANDRE adjusts her dress and leaves  but not before uttering the WORDS the NEW lord commander thought he 'd NEVER hear again you know nothing  JON SNOW END END 
BEGIN BEGIN later  STANNIS is in his chambers at CASTLE BLACK working on other letters  and SHIREEN enters END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS begins to apologise for dragging her along on campaign with him  as CASTLE BLACK is hardly a place for a child  but SHIREEN cuts him off she is happy to have COME  having expected to be left at DRAGONSTONE  as SELYSE had made it clear she wanted END END BEGIN BEGIN SHIREEN asks her father if he is ashamed of her because of her deformity STANNIS gets up from his table and explains that not LONG after SHIREEN was born  a DORNISH trader arrived on DRAGONSTONE and  having heard of SHIREEN 'S birth  gave a wooden doll as a GIFT for the newborn girl END END BEGIN BEGIN unfortunately  the doll was contaminated with greyscale  and by the time that was discovered  SHIREEN had already contracted the disease END END BEGIN BEGIN everyone claimed SHIREEN would DIE of it sooner or later  and urged STANNIS to send her to the ruins of VALYRIA to live out her days with the STONE MEN before the disease infected the rest of the CASTLE STANNIS says he told them all to go to hell and summoned every healer  apothecary and maester he could to save SHIREEN END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS insists that SHIREEN is his daughter and he would not send her away because she belonged with her family END END BEGIN BEGIN SHIREEN  overjoyed at her father 's declaration  runs over and gives him a hug which  after an awkward pause  STANNIS returns END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at WINTERFELL  SANSA STARK takes the opportunity to visit her family 's underground crypts END END BEGIN BEGIN she COMES to the tomb and statue of her aunt LYANNA STARK and finds the feather token that ROBERT BARATHEON left there years ago when he visited the CASTLE  END END BEGIN BEGIN PETYR BAELISH arrives and says he thought he 'd find her there END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA remarks that her father  EDDARD STARK  NEVER talked about LYANNA  but she would at times find him down in the crypts lighting candles at her tomb END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA NEVER knew LYANNA because she died before she was born  but she notes that people say she was beautiful END END 
BEGIN BEGIN LITTLEFINGER says that he actually saw LYANNA once years ago  and she was as beautiful as everyone says END END BEGIN BEGIN back when he was a BOY living with SANSA 'S MOTHER 'S family  the OLD lord whent of HARRENHAL held a massive tournament every notable figure of the time came from across WESTEROS the MAD king  CROWN PRINCE RHAEGAR TARGARYEN  ROBERT BARATHEON  LYANNA STARK  everyone END END BEGIN BEGIN LYANNA had already been publicly betrothed to ROBERT at the time END END BEGIN BEGIN BAELISH REMEMBERS how awed he was  a BOY from nowhere and with no significant holdings  to see all of these living legends gathered in one place END END BEGIN BEGIN in the final tilt  PRINCE RHAEGAR rode against ser BARRISTAN SELMY END END BEGIN BEGIN RHAEGAR won and the entire crowd erupted in cheers only to suddenly drop DEAD SILENT when RHAEGAR rode right past his wife  ELIA MARTELL  to lay the victor 's CROWN made of blue WINTER ROSES in LYANNA 'S lap END END BEGIN BEGIN not LONG AFTERWARDS  RHAEGAR made off with LYANNA  sparking off ROBERT 'S REBELLION which overthrew the TARGARYEN dynasty END END BEGIN BEGIN LITTLEFINGER wonders how many thousands died because RHAEGAR chose LYANNA to which SANSA says that he chose her  then kidnapped and raped her END END BEGIN BEGIN BAELISH gives her a wry look and moves on to another part of the crypts END END 
BEGIN BEGIN SANSA notices that LITTLEFINGER is wearing riding clothes  and he explains that he is heading back to king 's LANDING  because CERSEI sent a letter requesting his presence and it would be best not to make her suspicious by refusing to COME END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA will be alone with the BOLTONS but he explains his plan to her STANNIS will have to attack the BOLTONS soon if he is to beat the WINTER SNOWS  and he bets that STANNIS will probably WIN  because he is one of the best military commanders in all of WESTEROS  and the BOLTONS will be outnumbered by STANNIS  as the other NORTHERN HOUSES would be quick to betray their liege lord END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS will then make SANSA the NEW ruler of the NORTH  as the LAST known surviving STARK heir and in memory of her father EDDARD 'S support for STANNIS END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA asks what will happen on the off chance that STANNIS gets killed  and LITTLEFINGER explains that marrying RAMSAY BOLTON now will at least leave SANSA in a position to insinuate herself among the BOLTONS and help destroy them from within in future plans END END BEGIN BEGIN either way  SANSA will be LITTLEFINGER 'S powerful ally in the NORTH END END BEGIN BEGIN LITTLEFINGER kisses SANSA on the lips  and departs END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in MEEREEN  DAENERYS TARGARYEN is looking down on the streets below from her royal apartments in the GREAT pyramid  and ser BARRISTAN SELMY also brings up RHAEGAR TARGARYEN END END BEGIN BEGIN he says that the CITY 'S inhabitants always seem happy from such a distance  but RHAEGAR actually liked to leave the RED KEEP and mingle with the common people on the streets END END BEGIN BEGIN BARRISTAN accompanied him often to guard him  and says that RHAEGAR liked to sing to people END END BEGIN BEGIN he was a GREAT singer  so he would find a place on one of the streets just like any public minstrel and sing END END BEGIN BEGIN he liked to see how much money he could make  and everyone enjoyed his singing  so he often made quite a lot END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS is surprised  because her brother VISERYS only told her that RHAEGAR was a GREAT killer END END BEGIN BEGIN  END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  an injured GREY WORM continues to fight the SONS of the HARPY END END 
BEGIN BEGIN BARRISTAN scoffs that RHAEGAR was a GREAT warrior but NEVER enjoyed killing  he was a gentle MAN who enjoyed singing END END BEGIN BEGIN she asks what they did with all the money  and BARRISTAN says that they did all sorts of THINGS sometimes they just gave it to the next minstrel on the road  once RHAEGAR gave it all to an orphanage in the slums of FLEA BOTTOM  and one time they spent it to get horribly drunk END END BEGIN BEGIN DAARIO NAHARIS then COMES to say that the day 's supplicants are waiting in the THRONE room  chief among them HIZDAHR zo LORAQ END END BEGIN BEGIN aware of his dislike of politics  DAENERYS asks if BARRISTAN wants to attend her in the THRONE room after being assured that DAARIO has her back  she gives him the day off  cheerfully telling him to make some music in the CITY below END END 
BEGIN BEGIN HIZDAHR again beseeches DAENERYS to reopen the fighting PITS of MEEREEN  because today is the traditional beginning of the fighting SEASON END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS again refuses  but HIZDAHR rationally argues that the fighting PITS provide a GREAT spectacle that has always been enjoyed by both the slave MASTERS and slaves  and is one of the few THINGS that can bring the CITY together END END BEGIN BEGIN bringing back this major tradition will not instantly solve all of her problems  he concedes  but it would be a start at mending together her subjects END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as he speaks  the SONS of the HARPY are already mounting a series of large scale attacks in the streets END END BEGIN BEGIN a meereenese prostitute helps them distract and KILL some of the SECOND SONS  and when a patrol of UNSULLIED arrives  she feigns fear and directs them into a trap by pointing that the SONS of the HARPY ran into a NARROW alleyway END END BEGIN BEGIN the UNSULLIED give chase  only to be surrounded by a much larger number of the SONS of the HARPY END END BEGIN BEGIN brutal fighting rages throughout the streets of MEEREEN END END BEGIN BEGIN GREY WORM is among the ambushed UNSULLIED he KILLS many attackers  though he loses his helmet  is slashed in the leg  and is stabbed in his side END END BEGIN BEGIN GREY WORM pulls the dagger out of himself  stabs a foe in the throat with it  and KEEPS fighting  though his wounds slow him considerably END END BEGIN BEGIN most of the SONS of the HARPY are DEAD but they outnumber the UNSULLIED so much to begin with that only GREY WORM is left END END BEGIN BEGIN just then  ser BARRISTAN arrives and saves GREY WORM by drawing the attention of the remaining rebels END END BEGIN BEGIN he takes on eight SONS of the HARPY and defeats them all  save for the LAST one  who stabs him in the belly END END BEGIN BEGIN he falls to his knees and just as his attacker is about to slit his throat  GREY WORM takes him out by shoving his spear into his back END END BEGIN BEGIN GREY WORM staggers over BARRISTAN  but he has lost consciousness END END BEGIN BEGIN severely wounded  GREY WORM then slumps down to the floor next to him END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  SONS of the HARPY is the fourth EPISODE of the fifth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the forty fourth EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on MAY 3  2015 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by dave hill  and directed by mark mylod END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the FAITH MILITANT grow increasingly aggressive JAIME and BRONN head SOUTH ELLARIA and the SAND SNAKES vow vengeance END END 
BEGIN BEGIN MISSANDEI DAENERYS watches on as her DRAGONS set a head of GREAT family on FIRE and proceed to eat him END END BEGIN BEGIN watches over the wounded GREY WORM  who is still unconscious from his wounds sustained by the SONS of the HARPY END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS and DAARIO NAHARIS wake over the deceased ser BARRISTAN SELMY END END BEGIN BEGIN HIZDAHR zo LORAQ enters to extend his condolences END END BEGIN BEGIN DAARIO suggests pulling back around the pyramid to use it as a base from which to eradicate the SONS of the HARPY END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS instead opts for rounding up the leaders of each GREAT family in MEEREEN  including HIZDAHR END END BEGIN BEGIN the leaders are brought to the catacombs where RHAEGAL and viserion are chained up END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS 'S UNSULLIED push the leaders slowly towards the TWO DRAGONS  who can be heard growling from the darkness END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS states that good MOTHERS do not give up on their CHILDREN  they discipline them if needed  but NEVER give up on them END END BEGIN BEGIN she nods to DAARIO to push one of the leaders further forward END END BEGIN BEGIN a stream of FIRE COMING from RHAEGAL sets the MAN aflame before he is torn apart and eaten by both DRAGONS END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS suggests that the DRAGONS MAY determine the innocence of the captives and touches HIZDAHR 'S back as if she wanted to push him but then she pretends she wants not to overfeed the DRAGONS and lets the rest of the MEN be led away END END 
BEGIN BEGIN GREY WORM wakes up later with MISSANDEI sitting beside him END END BEGIN BEGIN he asks if BARRISTAN SELMY survived the attack by the SONS of the HARPY but MISSANDEI shakes her head END END BEGIN BEGIN GREY WORM thinks he has failed ser BARRISTAN  his MEN and DAENERYS a claim MISSANDEI denies END END BEGIN BEGIN MISSANDEI tells him he shouldn 't be ashamed for being wounded given that he was ambushed and outnumbered  but GREY WORM says he is ashamed that he was afraid when he was stabbed END END BEGIN BEGIN MISSANDEI says that everyone fears death END END BEGIN BEGIN however  GREY WORM says it isn 't death he fears  it is the thought of NEVER getting to see MISSANDEI again that terrified him END END BEGIN BEGIN MISSANDEI is noticeably touched and kisses GREY WORM END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS asks MISSANDEI whether she should reopen the fighting PITS END END BEGIN BEGIN MISSANDEI only says that she has seen DAENERYS listening to her counselors when her own experience was lacking and ignoring them when she thought they were wrong END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS visits the imprisoned HIZDAHR  who begs for his life END END BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS tells him she has decided to reopen the fighting PITS  but only for FREE MEN END END BEGIN BEGIN she also says that she will marry the head of an ancient family of MEEREEN to forge a bond with the people of the CITY  and that she luckily has one of them on his knees already END END BEGIN BEGIN she leaves a very confused HIZDAHR to ponder that he will live  and that he will soon be MEEREEN 'S PRINCE consort END END 
BEGIN BEGIN maester AEMON SAM reads a note from SLAVER 'S BAY to maester AEMON updating him on DAENERYS 'S situation END END BEGIN BEGIN SAM praises DAENERYS 'S courage but maester AEMON worries about his GREAT niece 's safety because she is all alone  under SIEGE  and with hardly anyone to guide her  while her LAST relation is useless and dying thousands of miles away END END BEGIN BEGIN JON SNOW enters to speak with AEMON in private END END BEGIN BEGIN he needs the maester 's advice on a controversial order that many of the NIGHT 'S WATCH will hate him for END END BEGIN BEGIN AEMON tells JON that half the MEN at CASTLE BLACK already hate him  but that he should trust in his command END END BEGIN BEGIN he says that JON will not enjoy being lord commander  but with luck  he MAY find the strength to do what needs to be done END END BEGIN BEGIN JON is told to KILL the BOY  and let the MAN be born END END

BEGIN BEGIN MELISANDRE begins praying and announces that they offer up the life of this girl to the lord of LIGHT  and sets the pyre on FIRE END END BEGIN BEGIN as she explained to STANNIS before  she believes that sacrificing SHIREEN 'S life which contains the power of a king 's BLOOD will gain the lord of LIGHT 'S favor  who in return will aid them in their time of need by lifting the blizzard END END BEGIN BEGIN STANNIS believes that if they do nothing  they will remain snowbound and all starve to death here END END BEGIN BEGIN SHIREEN continues to repeatedly cry MOTHER  please and father  please eventually even SELYSE  who only had a cold and non existent relationship with her daughter  suddenly breaks and rushes forward  begging that they can 't go through with it END END BEGIN BEGIN soldiers restrain her  however  and she sinks to the ground crying in despair END END BEGIN BEGIN SHIREEN 'S cries become even more frightened  but STANNIS continues to WATCH even as SELYSE sobs on the ground END END BEGIN BEGIN as the flames begin to consume SHIREEN she wordlessly screams in pain and fear  and eventually even STANNIS cannot BEAR to look anymore as she burns to death END END

BEGIN BEGIN  OATHBREAKER is the third EPISODE of the sixth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the fifty third EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on MAY 8  2016 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS  and directed by daniel sackheim END END

BEGIN BEGIN underneath the GREAT SEPT of BAELOR  SEPTA UNELLA enters queen MARGAERY TYRELL 'S cell and leads her to a private meeting with the HIGH SPARROW END END BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SPARROW asks her what she would do if he allowed her to leave that day END END BEGIN BEGIN MARGAERY replied that she wants to return to her family and her husband TOMMEN BARATHEON END END BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SPARROW respects her love for her family but tells her that attachment leads to sin  citing his experience as a cobbler END END BEGIN BEGIN MARGAERY manages to impress the SPARROW with her knowledge of the BOOK of the STRANGER  which she admits SEPTA UNELLA had read at her END END BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SPARROW chuckles and agrees that UNELLA has a habit of reading at people instead of to them END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the HIGH SPARROW recounts how in his youth he was a womanizer and drunkard END END BEGIN BEGIN he underwent a conversion experience the morning after an orgy  as his drunken guests lay naked all around his HOUSE END END BEGIN BEGIN tired of what he was now perceiving as a meaningless existence  the HIGH SPARROW then turned his life around and became a devoted member of the FAITH of the SEVEN END END BEGIN BEGIN he then left his job as a cobbler and devoted his life to the poor and destitute END END BEGIN BEGIN believing he has found a way to reach MARGAERY  the SPARROW allows her to visit her brother LORAS TYRELL END END

BEGIN BEGIN  BOOK of the STRANGER is the fourth EPISODE of the sixth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the fifty fourth EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on MAY 15  2016 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS  and directed by daniel sackheim END END 
BEGIN BEGIN TYRION strikes a deal END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH and DAARIO undertake a difficult task END END BEGIN BEGIN JAIME and CERSEI try to improve their situation END END BEGIN BEGIN JON and SANSA reunite END END 
BEGIN BEGIN SANSA STARK receives a message bearing the sigil of HOUSE BAELISH  asking her to a meeting in MOLE 'S TOWN END END BEGIN BEGIN accompanied by BRIENNE  SANSA furiously confronts PETYR BAELISH  asking if he was aware what RAMSAY BOLTON was capable of END END BEGIN BEGIN BAELISH deflects  saying he has the KNIGHTS of the VALE waiting at MOAT CAILIN to aid SANSA END END BEGIN BEGIN she is mistrustful of him when he claims he had no idea of RAMSAY 'S abusive treatment of her END END BEGIN BEGIN she doubts BAELISH 'S ability to protect her or even himself  threatening to have BRIENNE KILL him END END BEGIN BEGIN he says he 'll do whatever she asks and SANSA tells him to leave and NEVER COME back for her END END BEGIN BEGIN he obeys  but not before informing that her GREAT uncle BRYNDEN TULLY has recaptured RIVERRUN and recommending she seek him out and the remaining loyal TULLY forces END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA says she already has an ARMY  her brother JON SNOW 'S ARMY of WILDLINGS END END BEGIN BEGIN half brother  BAELISH clarifies as he WALKS away  reminding her that JON is only her half brother END END 
BEGIN BEGIN at CASTLE BLACK  a war COUNCIL is called  and is attended by SANSA  BRIENNE  PODRICK  JON  DAVOS  MELISANDRE  TORMUND and EDDISON tollett  who discuss the need for more MEN to defend CASTLE BLACK  since the KARSTARKS and UMBERS  TWO major HOUSES in the NORTH  have declared for RAMSAY END END BEGIN BEGIN JON points out that they can summon the rest of the minor HOUSES  such as the MORMONTS  glovers  cerwyns  and mazins  to rival their enemies  and SANSA reveals BRYNDEN 'S successful retaking of RIVERRUN  though she claims she learned via one of RAMSAY 'S RAVENS in order to stop JON from pursuing LITTLEFINGER END END BEGIN BEGIN SANSA subsequently tasks BRIENNE and PODRICK with securing BRYNDEN 'S help while the rest of them leave CASTLE BLACK to start building their ARMY END END BEGIN BEGIN before leaving CASTLE BLACK  SANSA presents JON with a NEW cloak like their father 's  carrying the STARK sigil END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the WAIF continues to drill ARYA  mocking her HIGH born origins END END BEGIN BEGIN JAQEN h ghar explains that the FACELESS MEN were slaves in VALYRIA before establishing the FREE CITY of BRAAVOS and the HOUSE of BLACK WHITE END END BEGIN BEGIN handing ARYA a vial  JAQEN tells her an actress  lady CRANE  will be the next to receive the many faced GOD s GIFT END END BEGIN BEGIN  END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  ARYA watches the bloody HAND  a stage play in BRAAVOS loosely based on the recent civil WARS in WESTEROS END END 
BEGIN BEGIN ARYA enjoys the spectacle of the actors re enacting the war of the FIVE KINGS  playing BARATHEONS and LANNISTERS  but her pleasure ceases when her father  and his execution  are inaccurately caricatured END END BEGIN BEGIN EDDARD is portrayed as a buffoon  and the actress who plays SANSA has her breasts bared to the audience END END BEGIN BEGIN ARYA sneaks into the dressing room after the play to observe her target the actress playing CERSEI who appears to be a clever  decent WOMAN END END BEGIN BEGIN ARYA later shares with JAQEN her plan to poison lady CRANE s rum  which no one else in the troupe drinks END END BEGIN BEGIN ARYA suspects that a jealous younger actress  bianca  has commissioned the KILL END END BEGIN BEGIN JAQEN cuts her off  reminding her a servant does not question END END 
BEGIN BEGIN DAENERYS is unsure of what to do with JORAH  having banished him twice  seeing him defiantly return twice  and him twice saving her life END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH finally confesses his love for DAENERYS  but also reveals his spreading greyscale infection  and says that this time  he needs to leave for good END END BEGIN BEGIN he starts to leave and states his plan to take his own life well before the greyscale envelops him  but DAENERYS tearfully commands him to find a cure and COME back to her side when she CONQUERS WESTEROS END END BEGIN BEGIN JORAH then departs while DAENERYS and DAARIO NAHARIS lead the DOTHRAKI horde back to MEEREEN END END 
BEGIN BEGIN while the rulers of MEEREEN enjoy a tenuous peace  TYRION reminds them of the need to convince the meereenese that everything has been done with DAENERYS 'S blessing  as the MASTERS could use TYRION and VARYS 'S foreign status against them to reclaim SLAVER 'S BAY END END BEGIN BEGIN to that END  TYRION invites KINVARA  HIGH PRIESTESS of the RED temple of VOLANTIS  to negotiate spreading the word of DAENERYS 'S accomplishments END END BEGIN BEGIN to TYRION 'S surprise  KINVARA appears to be highly accommodating in supporting TYRION 'S goals  as she firmly believes that DAENERYS is the PRINCE that was promised END END BEGIN BEGIN VARYS is more skeptical  being suspicious of any practitioners of magic  and points out that MELISANDRE had already declared STANNIS BARATHEON to be the PRINCE  only for him to be defeated twice END END BEGIN BEGIN KINVARA says that while the lord of LIGHT has a plan  the humans following him do occasionally make errors END END BEGIN BEGIN she then unnerves VARYS by revealing that she knows VARYS was emasculated by a SECOND rate sorcerer and offers to repeat the WORDS he heard in the flames  and identify who it was that spoke END END BEGIN BEGIN VARYS is uncharacteristically unsettled by this revelation END END BEGIN BEGIN KINVARA then assures TYRION that she will send the preachers and priests best suited to the task at HAND END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as the kingsmoot is held  YARA GREYJOY is the FIRST to lay claim to the SALT THRONE END END BEGIN BEGIN YARA argues that raiding the mainland is not enough for their people  and that they need to use military force to teach the mainlanders a lesson END END BEGIN BEGIN an IRONBORN MAN challenges YARA 'S candidacy on the grounds that she is a WOMAN and points out that her brother THEON GREYJOY has returned END END BEGIN BEGIN THEON endorses his older sister and urges the gathering to do the same stressing that she is a warrior  a reaver  and an IRONBORN END END BEGIN BEGIN many shout for YARA to be their queen END END 
BEGIN BEGIN before they can CROWN YARA  EURON GREYJOY joins the gathering to lay claim to the SALT THRONE END END BEGIN BEGIN he openly mocks THEON for his military failures and emasculation before deriding YARA as a WOMAN END END BEGIN BEGIN YARA in turn accuses EURON of killing their king and her father BALON END END BEGIN BEGIN to her surprise  EURON admits killing BALON but then defends his actions on the grounds that BALON was leading them to defeat in the NORTH END END BEGIN BEGIN when EURON states that his only regret is not killing BALON years earlier  he is met by resounding cheers from the crowd END END BEGIN BEGIN THEON then counters that EURON had spent years gallivanting overseas while YARA was commanding IRONBORN ships and MEN END END BEGIN BEGIN YARA then suggests building a massive fleet to attack and make their mark on WESTEROS END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in response  EURON announces that he also supports expanding the IRONBORN fleet END END BEGIN BEGIN revealing a trick up his sleeve  he then proposes to marry DAENERYS TARGARYEN and then carry her ARMY and DRAGONS back to WESTEROS END END BEGIN BEGIN the IRONBORN support EURON 'S plan and declare him king END END BEGIN BEGIN the DROWNED MEN priest AERON GREYJOY then leads EURON down to the SEA to be DROWNED and reborn  as is the custom END END BEGIN BEGIN knowing that EURON will KILL them as soon as he is able  YARA  THEON  and many of their loyalists flee the IRON ISLANDS during EURON 'S coronation  taking much of the IRON fleet with them END END BEGIN BEGIN after EURON revives himself  he is crowned by his brother AERON END END BEGIN BEGIN after learning that his niece and nephew have fled with their best ships  EURON calls on his followers to build their own ships so that he MAY pursue the pair and KILL them END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the THREE EYED RAVEN shows BRAN a vision of a heart tree amid spirals of standing STONES in a lush green valley END END BEGIN BEGIN his vision shows LEAF and other CHILDREN of the FOREST talking amongst themselves  then looking eagerly at a captive bound to the tree END END BEGIN BEGIN LEAF approaches and forces a dragonglass dagger into the captive 's chest END END BEGIN BEGIN the captive screams  but does not DIE  instead becoming the FIRST WHITE WALKER END END 
BEGIN BEGIN BRAN immediately confronts LEAF about creating the WHITE WALKERS in the FIRST place END END BEGIN BEGIN LEAF tries to explain that they were at war with the FIRST MEN and were desperate END END BEGIN BEGIN later  BRAN is the only one in the cave awake and is anxious to warg back into the WEIRWOOD tree END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN wargs into the tree by himself and sees the ARMY of the DEAD END END BEGIN BEGIN he slowly WALKS through the ARMY until he COMES to a space occupied by four WHITE WALKERS  including the NIGHT king END END BEGIN BEGIN as BRAN becomes aware that the the NIGHT king and the DEAD are now able to see him  the NIGHT king grabs his arm  branding him with an icy mark END END BEGIN BEGIN he breaks out of the vision with a scream waking the others END END BEGIN BEGIN the THREE EYED RAVEN tells BRAN  MEERA and HODOR that the NIGHT king is now able to locate BRAN and able to bypass the powerful magic keeping the WHITE WALKERS and the wights out of the cave END END BEGIN BEGIN as a result  they must leave now and BRAN must become the THREE EYED RAVEN END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN asks whether he is ready  and the RAVEN says no at which point BRAN 'S eyes whiten as he enters another vision END END 
BEGIN BEGIN as MEERA and HODOR are preparing to leave they notice the air is so cold their breath is visible  indicating the arrival of the ARMY of the DEAD OUTSIDE of the cave END END BEGIN BEGIN the NIGHT king and THREE WHITE WALKERS start marching towards the cave END END BEGIN BEGIN the CHILDREN of the FOREST try using magic projectiles to fend the WALKERS off  but are overwhelmed END END BEGIN BEGIN they LIGHT a FIRE around the entrance which prevents the wights from entering but the WALKERS extinguish a pathway and WALK through END END BEGIN BEGIN the wights END up climbing over the WEIRWOOD and dropping through roots at the top of the cave END END BEGIN BEGIN MEERA desperately tries to get BRAN out of the vision and attempts to get the frightened HODOR to carry BRAN away to no avail END END BEGIN BEGIN using a dragonglass tipped spear  MEERA KILLS the FIRST WHITE WALKER that enters  and fights alongside the remaining CHILDREN of the FOREST to try to fend off the wights until BRAN wakes up END END BEGIN BEGIN wights begin to swarm the cave  killing all of the CHILDREN of the FOREST except for LEAF  as MEERA starts yelling at BRAN to warg into HODOR END END 
BEGIN BEGIN in the vision  BRAN is at WINTERFELL watching NED STARK say goodbye to his father  RICKARD STARK  before being sent to the VALE as a ward END END BEGIN BEGIN while still in the vision  BRAN hears MEERA 'S cries to warg into HODOR and the THREE EYED RAVEN tells him to listen to her END END BEGIN BEGIN BRAN wargs into both the present day HODOR in the cave and WYLIS  the young version of HODOR in his vision END END 
BEGIN BEGIN  WYLIS seizing  as his WORDS HOLD the DOOR evolve into HODOR  END END 
BEGIN BEGIN the HODOR in the cave puts BRAN 'S body on a sled and starts hauling him down a tunnel leading out of the cave with LEAF and MEERA  as BRAN 'S direwolf SUMMER is killed attacking the wights END END BEGIN BEGIN as the wights are closing in on them  LEAF sacrifices herself  using magic to cause a huge explosion  buying the other THREE enough time to get to a DOOR at the END of the tunnel END END BEGIN BEGIN while the THREE EYED RAVEN and BRAN are still sharing a vision  the NIGHT king KILLS the THREE EYED RAVEN  and his figure within BRAN 'S vision blows away as ashes and rags END END 
BEGIN BEGIN with some difficulty HODOR pushes the DOOR open and pulls BRAN through  COMING back to help MEERA close the DOOR just as the wights approach END END BEGIN BEGIN MEERA grabs BRAN 'S sled and tells HODOR to bar the exit  shouting to HOLD the DOOR  END END BEGIN BEGIN inside BRAN 'S vision  WYLIS notices BRAN  who links the present HODOR to the past WYLIS END END BEGIN BEGIN WYLIS begins to seize when he enters the mind of his future self END END BEGIN BEGIN as MEERA continues to yell HOLD the DOOR to present day HODOR  within BRAN 'S vision WYLIS falls to the ground convulsing and starts repeating this same sentence in the midst of his seizure END END BEGIN BEGIN eventually  HOLD the DOOR slurs into HODOR  as his condition deteriorates and it becomes apparent this is the moment HODOR lost the ability to say any other WORDS  and his destiny was fixed END END 
BEGIN BEGIN present day HODOR braces himself against the DOOR LONG enough for MEERA to disappear into the SNOW with BRAN 'S unconscious body on the sled END END BEGIN BEGIN inevitably  the wights break through parts of the WOOD and begin scratching and stabbing a visibly distressed HODOR END END BEGIN BEGIN with no possibility of escape  all that is shown at the END is young WYLIS in the past seizing and crying out HODOR END END BEGIN BEGIN  END END
BEGIN BEGIN  the DOOR is the fifth EPISODE of the sixth SEASON of GAME OF THRONES END END BEGIN BEGIN it is the fifty fifth EPISODE of the series overall END END BEGIN BEGIN it premiered on MAY 22  2016 END END BEGIN BEGIN it was written by DAVID BENIOFF and D.B END END BEGIN BEGIN WEISS  and directed by jack bender END END
